Changes 5 With the Core UI split completed it is now possible to build Gaim 6 without any UIs creating a libgaim library upon which other UIs 7 may be constructed 8 A new ncurses based console UI called gaim text is now available 9 Sadrul Habib Chowdhury Google Summer of Code 1 Reorganized the source tree to split apart the code for the UI 11 changes and libgaim targets 12 libxml2 is now required We switched from gmarkup to libxml2 for 13 more correct XML parsing 14 415 Status System 516 The code dealing with buddy and account status away messages 1324 1425 Buddy List 26 Performance when manipulating and displaying the buddy list has 27 been significantly improved Aaron Sheldon Google Summer of Code 1528 Buddy icons are now shown in tooltips Felipe Contreras 1629 Tooltips now contain additional information about a Person that 2134 will remain hidden when Gaim is started again Scott Shedden 2235 Improved buddy list searching with CTRL F 36 Ability to set a buddy icon for all of your accounts at once via 37 the buddy list You can still set per account icons via the 38 account editor 39 The space wasted by the group expanders has been eliminated and 4 the expander setting in gtkrc 2 is no longer needed 2341 2442 Conversations and Chats 5472 as Plain Text hit Ctrl R after pasting or use the Clear Formatting 5573 button on the toolbar 74 Performance while joining large chat rooms has been significantly 75 improved Aaron Sheldon Google Summer of Code 5676 5777 Sounds 5878 Beautiful new default sounds Brad Turcotte 59 Use libao for playing sounds via NAS instead of accessing NAS directly 79 Use GStreamer for playing sounds instead of libao 6 8 A volume control in the preferences Casey Harkins 6181 1 12 Highlight when nick said option added to Message get patches 31against the absolute latest SVN I get really annoyed when I get patches 3232against the last released version especially since I don t usually have 3333a copy of it on my computer and gaim tends to change a lot between 34 versions I sometimes get annoyed when they re against CVS from 3 days 34versions I sometimes get annoyed when they re against SVN from 3 days 3535ago but can t complain because it s usually my fault that I haven t 36 looked at the patch yet To get gaim from CVS if you haven t already 36looked at the patch yet To get gaim from SVN if you haven t already 3737run the following commands 3838 39 export CVSROOT pserver anonymous cvs sourceforge net cvsroot gaim 4 cvs login hit enter as the password 41 cvs co gaim you ll see it getting all of the files 39 svn co https svn sourceforge net svnroot gaim trunk gaim 424 cd gaim 4341 autogen sh 4543You ll now have your normal gaim tree with configure and all which 4644 autogen sh takes the liberty of running for you If you want to make 47 your life really simple learn how CVS works CVS is your friend To make 45your life really simple learn how SVN works SVN is your friend To make 4846a patch just edit the files right there in that tree don t bother with 4947two trees or even two copies of the same file Then when you re ready to 5 make your patch simply run cvs diff u my patch and post it on 48make your
